      "keystrokes": "cat > /app/debug_simple.py << 'ENDSCRIPT'\nimport sys\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\nfrom feal import getleft, getright, merge, f_function\nimport random\n\n# Use known keys\nrandom.seed(42)\nkeys = []\nfor i in range(6):\n    x = random.randint(0, 0xFFFF)\n    keys.append((x * 1234567) & 0xFFFFFFFF)\n\nprint(f\"Keys: {[hex(k) for k in keys]}\")\nprint(f\"key[5] = {hex(keys[5])}\")\nprint()\n\ndef encrypt_with_keys(plaintext):\n    left = getleft(plaintext)\n    right = getright(plaintext)\n    left ^= keys[0]\n    right ^= keys[1]\n    right ^= left\n    for round_num in range(4):\n        mixed = f_function(right ^ keys[round_num + 2])\n        temp = right\n        right = left ^ mixed\n        left = temp\n    left ^= right\n    return merge(right, left)\n\n# Choose a pair with same (left ^ right)\nleft_a = 0x00000000\nright_a = 0x00000000  # X = 0\n\nleft_b = 0x12345678\nright_b = 0x12345678  # X = 0\n\nP_a = merge(left_a, right_a)\nP_b = merge(left_b, right_b)\n\nC_a = encrypt_with_keys(P_a)\nC_b = encrypt_with_keys(P_b)\n\nprint(f\"P_a: {hex(P_a)} -> C_a: {hex(C_a)}\")\nprint(f\"P_b: {hex(P_b)} -> C_b: {hex(C_b)}\")\nprint()\n\n# Test the simpler equation: L3_1 ^ L3_2 = left1 ^ left2\nk5 = keys[5]\n\nR3_a = getright(C_a) ^ getleft(C_a)\nR3_b = getright(C_b) ^ getleft(C_b)\n\nL3_a = getleft(C_a) ^ f_function(R3_a ^ k5)\nL3_b = getleft(C_b) ^ f_function(R3_b ^ k5)\n\ndelta = left_a ^ left_b\nprint(f\"left_a ^ left_b = {hex(delta)}\")\nprint(f\"L3_a ^ L3_b = {hex(L3_a ^ L3_b)}\")\nprint(f\"Match (should be True for correct k5): {L3_a ^ L3_b == delta}\")\nprint()\n\n# Now test with a WRONG k5\nwrong_k5 = k5 ^ 1  #
